<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vaten.html>vaten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vaten.html>vaten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*faton</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fatÅnÄ</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vat.html>vat</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>. The short <i>a</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> introduced by analogy with the uninflected singular form of the noun <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vat.html>vat</a></i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vechter.html>vechter</a> (8165)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vechter.html>vechter</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vechter.html>vechters</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vechter.html>vechtertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">vechtster</b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:veehouder.html>veehouder</a> (86850)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vee.html>vee</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">livestock</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">to keep</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">denominative <a href = vnd.unilang:agent.html>agent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">agriculture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> someone who keeps livestock, a livestock farmer</li></ol>

***veel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> (114)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vele.html>vele</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:filo.html>filo</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*felu</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner_2">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>many, much, a lot of</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>As a determiner <i><a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a></i> typically isn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> inflected in informal Dutch. In formal style the inflected form <i><a href = vnd.unilang:vele.html>vele</a></i> may be used, but only for plurals or before (usually uncountable) singular nouns with a definite article:
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vele.html>Vele</a></b> rolstoelgebruikers <a href = vnd.unilang:hadden.html>hadden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bezwaren.html>bezwaren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plannen.html>plannen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Many</b> wheelchair users <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> objections against the plans.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vele.html>vele</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geweld.html>geweld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dreef.html>dreef</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:inwoners.html>inwoners</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weg.html>weg</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b>large amount</b> of violence drove inhabitants away.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>much, a lot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vanaf.html>Vanaf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zien.html>zien</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">From here I can see <b>a lot</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:veelal.html>veelal</a> (38771)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>1710; compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">much</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vraat</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">gobbling, eating gluttonously</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">VielfraÃ</i> or  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">Veelfraat</i>. The term originally meant simply âgluttonâ in German, but <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> applied to the <a href = vnd.unilang:hyena.html>hyena</a> in pre-modern times. In the 15th century, Old <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">fjellfross</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wolverine.html>wolverine</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">mountain cat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> borrowed into Middle Low German by Hanseatic fur traders as <i class="None mention" lang="mgl">villevrÄs</i> and folk-etymologically blended with the existing word for âgluttonâ, possibly influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Finnish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Finnish language">Finnish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fi">ahma</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">glutton; <a href = vnd.unilang:wolverine.html>wolverine</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, giving <i class="None mention" lang="mgl">veelvratz</i> (Reinke <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vos.html>Vos</a>, 1498), <i class="None mention" lang="mgl">vÄlevrÄs</i>, <i class="None mention" lang="mgl">vÄlevrÄt</i>. The meaning â<a href = vnd.unilang:wolverine.html>wolverine</a>â <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> initially the only one received into Dutch, although by 1849 the word <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> acquired the meaning âgluttonâ.
</p>

***veertien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:veertien.html>veertien</a> (3710)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">viertien</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:veertien.html>veertien</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*viurtÄn</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*viurtien</i>, *<i>fiortian</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fedurtehun</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">vierzehn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">fjirtjin</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fourteen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">fjorten</i>.
</p>

***veertiende.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:veertiende.html>veertiende</a> (14585)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veertiende.html>veertiende</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>fourteenth</li></ol>

***veertig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:veertig.html>veertig</a> (3060)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">viertich</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vÄertich</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*viertig</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fedwÅr tigiwiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral_2">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veertig.html>veertig</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>forty</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Although <a href = vnd.unilang:spelt.html>spelt</a> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">v-</i>, the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> traditionally pronounced with initial <span class="IPA">/f/</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> in accents that generally do not devoice <i>v-</i>. (This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> due to analogy with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeventig.html>zeventig</a></i> ["seventy"], which used to have a prefix <i>t-</i> and hence a devoiced <i>z-</i>.) However, there are also many <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a> who pronounce <span class="IPA">/v/</span> in line with the spelling. The WNT (1954) notes that the voiced pronunciation isn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> very common, while Auer and Hinskens state that this realisation <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> becoming increasingly common in Standard Dutch due to hypercorrection.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:veertig.html>veertig</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span> / <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

***vegetarisch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vegetarisch.html>vegetarisch</a> (17435)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vegetarisch.html>vegetarisch</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>vegetarian (relating to the type of diet eaten by vegetarians)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>While <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vegetariÃ«r</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the standard noun to refer to someone who follows a vegetarian diet, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:vegetarisch.html>vegetarisch</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also not uncommonly used to refer to people. Thus, "<a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vegetarisch.html>vegetarisch</a>?" (<i>are you vegetarian?</i>) might be used to ask someone if they eat a vegetarian diet instead of the more standard "<a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> vegetariÃ«r?" (<i>are you a vegetarian?</i>). However, since <i><a href = vnd.unilang:vegetarisch.html>vegetarisch</a></i> in standard Dutch refers only to food and not to the people who follow a vegetarian diet, this usage of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:vegetarisch.html>vegetarisch</a></i> to refer to people <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often considered incorrect.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vegetarisch.html>vegetarisch</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> vegetariÃ«rs
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> at <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vegetarisch.html>vegetarisch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:restaurant.html>restaurant</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Verwante_begrippen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:verwante.html>Verwante</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrippen.html>begrippen</a></i></span></h5>
<ul><li>vegetariÃ«r, vegetarisme, fruitarisch, <a href = vnd.unilang:vega.html>vega</a></li></ul>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veiligheid.html>veiligheid</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:speld.html>speld</a></i>, perhaps a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">safety pin</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vel.html>vel</a> (6761)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vel.html>vel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:fel.html>fel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fellÄ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pello-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pelno-</i>, whence Latin pellis, Greek ÏÎ­Î»Î»Î±; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Fell</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vel.html>vel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vellen.html>vellen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:velletje.html>velletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A skin, a hide.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>Haar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:velletje.html>velletje</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zat.html>zat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tussen.html>tussen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deur.html>deur</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Her <b>skin</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> caught in the <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A fur, a pelt.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tientallen.html>Tientallen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vellen.html>vellen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beren.html>beren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wolven.html>wolven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lagen.html>lagen</a> opeengestapeld.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Tens of <b>pelts</b> of <a href = vnd.unilang:bears.html>bears</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:wolves.html>wolves</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> stacked on each other.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A sheet (e.g. of paper; incorrectly used for a page).
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:glas.html>glas</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gloeilamp.html>gloeilamp</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dikker.html>dikker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vel.html>vel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:papier.html>papier</a></i>
<dl><dd><i>The glass of a lightbulb <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not much thicker than a </i>sheet<i> of paper.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>A membrane, e.g. forming on boiling milk.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:saus.html>saus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koken.html>koken</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:anders.html>anders</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontstaan.html>ontstaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vellen.html>vellen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This sauce shouldn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> boil for too long or else <b>membranes</b> will appear.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_4">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
